9-32 DECKLISTS
==============



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on March 12, 2017 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_meghanwolff_0.jpg)
By Meghan Wolff




 Meghan is one half of the podcast Magic the Amateuring and an adjunct professor at Tolarian Community College. She loves Limited, likes Modern, and dips her toes into each Standard season. She's decidedly blue and is the #1 hater of Siege Rhino in the Multiverse. 






Below are the decklists for players in places 9 through 32 at Grand Prix New Jersey. Readers interested in a new take on Standard should pore over Temur Dynavolt Tower decks from Seth Manfield, Oliver Tomajko, and Clay Gereffi, or Andrew Davis’s Esper Control deck.


*\*Unfortunately, we were unable to locate John Parker and Nate Sturm's decklists. Parker and Sturm finished 11th and 21st, respectively.*







#### Zachary Plott's Mardu Vehicles– GP New Jersey
